Parameter #1Parameter #2
def findMaxConsecutiveOnes(nums): max_count = 0 current_count = 0 for num in nums: if num == 1: current_count += 1 max_count = max(max_count, current_count) else: current_count = 0 return max_count nums2 = [1,0,1,1,0,1] print(findMaxConsecutiveOnes(nums2)) # Output: 22
